---

## 1. Executive Summary

**FooHut Dev** is where ideas become production-ready applications in minutes, not months. It's an AI-native development environment that deeply integrates with GitHub, letting you go from a napkin sketch to a deployed app with natural language and real-time collaboration.

### 1.1 The Vision

```

### 1.2 Core Differentiators

| bolt.new | FooHut Dev |
|----------|------------|
| Ephemeral projects | GitHub-native (real repos) |
| Single-file focus | Full project structure |
| Limited frameworks | Any stack, any language |
| Basic preview | Full dev server + terminal |
| No version control | Git built-in |
| Solo development | Real-time multiplayer |
| No CI/CD | GitHub Actions integrated |
| One deployment | Multi-environment |

## 7. Development Server & Preview

---

## 11. Database Schema

```sql
-- =====================================================
-- FOOHUT DEV CORE TABLES
-- =====================================================

-- Projects
CREATE TABLE dev_projects (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  owner_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  org_id TEXT REFERENCES organizations(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  -- Basic info
  name TEXT NOT NULL,
  slug TEXT NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  
  -- GitHub integration
  github_repo_id INTEGER,
  github_repo_full_name TEXT, -- e.g., "matto/project-manager"
  github_default_branch TEXT DEFAULT 'main',
  github_installation_id INTEGER,
  
  -- Framework detection
  detected_framework TEXT, -- 'nextjs', 'vite', 'express', etc.
  detected_language TEXT, -- 'typescript', 'javascript', 'python', etc.
  
  -- Settings
  settings TEXT DEFAULT '{}', -- JSON
  
  -- Status
  visibility TEXT DEFAULT 'private', -- 'private', 'public', 'unlisted'
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'active', -- 'active', 'archived', 'deleted'
  
  -- Timestamps
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  last_opened_at DATETIME,
  
  UNIQUE(owner_id, slug)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_dev_projects_owner ON dev_projects(owner_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_dev_projects_github ON dev_projects(github_repo_full_name);

-- Project collaborators
CREATE TABLE dev_project_collaborators (
  project_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES dev_projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  user_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  role TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'editor', -- 'owner', 'admin', 'editor', 'viewer'
  invited_by TEXT REFERENCES users(id),
  joined_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY(project_id, user_id)
);

-- Dev containers
CREATE TABLE dev_containers (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  project_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES dev_projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  -- Container info
  container_id TEXT, -- Docker/VM ID
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'stopped', -- 'creating', 'running', 'stopped', 'error'
  region TEXT DEFAULT 'us-west',
  
  -- Resources
  cpu_cores INTEGER DEFAULT 2,
  memory_mb INTEGER DEFAULT 4096,
  disk_gb INTEGER DEFAULT 20,
  
  -- Runtime
  base_image TEXT DEFAULT 'foohut/dev:latest',
  node_version TEXT,
  python_version TEXT,
  
  -- Ports
  forwarded_ports TEXT DEFAULT '[]', -- JSON array
  
  -- Timestamps
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  started_at DATETIME,
  last_activity_at DATETIME
);

CREATE INDEX idx_dev_containers_project ON dev_containers(project_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_dev_containers_status ON dev_containers(status);

-- Deployments
CREATE TABLE dev_deployments (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  project_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES dev_projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  -- Deploy info
  environment TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'production', 'staging', 'preview'
  provider TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'foohut', 'vercel', 'netlify', etc.
  
  -- Git info
  branch TEXT NOT NULL,
  commit_sha TEXT NOT NULL,
  commit_message TEXT,
  
  -- Status
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending', -- 'pending', 'building', 'deploying', 'live', 'failed', 'cancelled'
  
  -- URLs
  url TEXT,
  preview_url TEXT,
  
  -- Build info
  build_time_ms INTEGER,
  build_logs TEXT,
  
  -- Metadata
  deployed_by TEXT REFERENCES users(id),
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  completed_at DATETIME
);

CREATE INDEX idx_dev_deployments_project ON dev_deployments(project_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_dev_deployments_env ON dev_deployments(environment);

-- Environment variables
CREATE TABLE dev_env_variables (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  project_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES dev_projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  key TEXT NOT NULL,
  value TEXT NOT NULL, -- Encrypted
  
  -- Scopes
  environment TEXT DEFAULT 'all', -- 'all', 'production', 'staging', 'preview', 'development'
  
  -- Metadata
  created_by TEXT REFERENCES users(id),
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  
  UNIQUE(project_id, key, environment)
);

-- AI conversations in dev
CREATE TABLE dev_ai_conversations (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  project_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES dev_projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  user_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
  
  -- Conversation data
  messages TEXT NOT NULL, -- JSON array
  context TEXT, -- Files, selections, etc.
  
  -- Metrics
  tokens_used INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  
  -- Timestamps
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- File change history (for AI context)
CREATE TABLE dev_file_changes (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  project_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES dev_projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  file_path TEXT NOT NULL,
  change_type TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'create', 'update', 'delete', 'rename'
  
  -- Git info
  commit_sha TEXT,
  
  -- Change info
  lines_added INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  lines_removed INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  
  -- Metadata
  changed_by TEXT REFERENCES users(id),
  changed_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE INDEX idx_dev_file_changes_project ON dev_file_changes(project_id);

-- Real-time presence
CREATE TABLE dev_presence (
  project_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES dev_projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  user_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  -- Location
  file_path TEXT,
  cursor_line INTEGER,
  cursor_column INTEGER,
  selection TEXT, -- JSON for selection range
  
  -- Status
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'active', -- 'active', 'idle', 'away'
  activity TEXT, -- 'editing', 'viewing', 'terminal', etc.
  
  -- Timestamps
  last_seen_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  
  PRIMARY KEY(project_id, user_id)
);

-- GitHub webhooks
CREATE TABLE dev_github_webhooks (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  project_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES dev_projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  event_type TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'push', 'pull_request', 'issue', etc.
  payload TEXT NOT NULL, -- JSON
  
  -- Status
  processed BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  processed_at DATETIME,
  
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE INDEX idx_dev_webhooks_project ON dev_github_webhooks(project_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_dev_webhooks_processed ON dev_github_webhooks(processed);
```

---

## 12. API Endpoints

### 12.1 Project Endpoints

```
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects                    Create project
GET    /api/v1/dev/projects                    List my projects
GET    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id                Get project
PATCH  /api/v1/dev/projects/:id                Update project
DELETE /api/v1/dev/projects/:id                Delete project

POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/import             Import from GitHub
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/generate           Generate from AI prompt
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/fork           Fork project

GET    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/collaborators  List collaborators
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/collaborators  Add collaborator
PATCH  /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/collaborators/:uid Update role
DELETE /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/collaborators/:uid Remove collaborator
```

### 12.2 Container Endpoints

```
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/container/start    Start container
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/container/stop     Stop container
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/container/restart  Restart container
GET    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/container/status   Get container status
GET    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/container/logs     Get container logs

WS     /ws/dev/terminal/:id                        Terminal WebSocket
WS     /ws/dev/preview/:id                         Preview WebSocket
```

### 12.3 File System Endpoints

```
GET    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/files             List files
GET    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/files/*path       Get file content
PUT    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/files/*path       Write file
DELETE /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/files/*path       Delete file
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/files/rename      Rename file
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/files/upload      Upload files

WS     /ws/dev/files/:id                          Real-time file sync
```

### 12.4 Git Endpoints

```
GET    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/git/status        Git status
GET    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/git/branches      List branches
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/git/branches      Create branch
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/git/checkout      Checkout branch
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/git/commit        Commit changes
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/git/push          Push to remote
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/git/pull          Pull from remote
GET    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/git/diff          Get diff
GET    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/git/log           Get commit history
```

### 12.5 GitHub Integration Endpoints

```
GET    /api/v1/dev/github/repos                   List user repos
GET    /api/v1/dev/github/repos/:owner/:repo      Get repo details
GET    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/github/prs        List pull requests
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/github/prs        Create pull request
GET    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/github/issues     List issues
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/github/issues     Create issue
GET    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/github/actions    List workflow runs
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/github/actions/:id/rerun  Re-run workflow
```

### 12.6 Deployment Endpoints

```
GET    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/deployments       List deployments
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/deploy            Deploy project
GET    /api/v1/dev/deployments/:id                Get deployment
GET    /api/v1/dev/deployments/:id/logs           Get deployment logs
POST   /api/v1/dev/deployments/:id/cancel         Cancel deployment
POST   /api/v1/dev/deployments/:id/rollback       Rollback deployment

GET    /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/env               List env variables
POST   /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/env               Add env variable
PATCH  /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/env/:key          Update env variable
DELETE /api/v1/dev/projects/:id/env/:key          Delete env variable
```

### 12.7 AI Endpoints

```
POST   /api/v1/dev/ai/generate                    Generate code/files
POST   /api/v1/dev/ai/complete                    Code completion
POST   /api/v1/dev/ai/explain                     Explain code
POST   /api/v1/dev/ai/fix                         Fix errors
POST   /api/v1/dev/ai/refactor                    Refactor code
POST   /api/v1/dev/ai/test                        Generate tests
POST   /api/v1/dev/ai/docs                        Generate docs
POST   /api/v1/dev/ai/review                      Code review
POST   /api/v1/dev/ai/commit-message              Generate commit message
POST   /api/v1/dev/ai/pr-description              Generate PR description
POST   /api/v1/dev/ai/chat                        Chat with AI

WS     /ws/dev/ai/:id                             Streaming AI responses
```

### 12.8 Real-Time WebSocket

```
WS /ws/dev/project/:id

Messages:
â†’ presence:update      { file, cursor, selection }
â†’ file:change          { path, content, version }
â†’ file:create          { path, content }
â†’ file:delete          { path }
â†’ file:rename          { oldPath, newPath }
â†’ terminal:input       { data }
â†’ ai:request           { prompt, context }

â† presence:sync        { users: [...] }
â† file:changed         { path, content, version, user }
â† file:created         { path, user }
â† file:deleted         { path, user }
â† file:renamed         { oldPath, newPath, user }
â† terminal:output      { data }
â† ai:response          { content }
â† ai:stream            { chunk }
â† build:status         { status, logs }
â† deploy:status        { status, url }
```

## 14. Zustand Stores

```typescript
// stores/devProjectStore.ts
interface DevProjectStore {
  project: DevProject | null;
  container: ContainerStatus | null;
  files: FileTree;
  openFiles: string[];
  activeFile: string | null;
  
  // Actions
  loadProject: (id: string) => Promise<void>;
  startContainer: () => Promise<void>;
  stopContainer: () => Promise<void>;
  
  // File operations
  openFile: (path: string) => void;
  closeFile: (path: string) => void;
  createFile: (path: string, content?: string) => Promise<void>;
  updateFile: (path: string, content: string) => void;
  deleteFile: (path: string) => Promise<void>;
  renameFile: (oldPath: string, newPath: string) => Promise<void>;
}

// stores/devGitStore.ts
interface DevGitStore {
  status: GitStatus | null;
  branches: Branch[];
  currentBranch: string;
  stagedFiles: string[];
  changedFiles: string[];
  
  // Actions
  fetchStatus: () => Promise<void>;
  stageFile: (path: string) => void;
  unstageFile: (path: string) => void;
  stageAll: () => void;
  commit: (message: string) => Promise<void>;
  push: () => Promise<void>;
  pull: () => Promise<void>;
  checkout: (branch: string) => Promise<void>;
  createBranch: (name: string) => Promise<void>;
}

// stores/devGitHubStore.ts
interface DevGitHubStore {
  connected: boolean;
  repos: Repository[];
  pullRequests: PullRequest[];
  issues: Issue[];
  actions: WorkflowRun[];
  
  // Actions
  connect: () => Promise<void>;
  fetchRepos: () => Promise<void>;
  fetchPRs: () => Promise<void>;
  createPR: (data: CreatePRData) => Promise<PullRequest>;
  mergePR: (id: number) => Promise<void>;
  fetchIssues: () => Promise<void>;
  createIssue: (data: CreateIssueData) => Promise<Issue>;
  fetchActions: () => Promise<void>;
  rerunAction: (id: number) => Promise<void>;
}

// stores/devDeployStore.ts
interface DevDeployStore {
  deployments: Deployment[];
  environments: Environment[];
  envVariables: EnvVariable[];
  domains: CustomDomain[];
  
  // Actions
  deploy: (env: string, branch: string) => Promise<Deployment>;
  cancelDeploy: (id: string) => Promise<void>;
  rollback: (id: string) => Promise<void>;
  fetchDeployments: () => Promise<void>;
  addEnvVariable: (key: string, value: string, env: string) => Promise<void>;
  addDomain: (domain: string, env: string) => Promise<void>;
}

// stores/devAIStore.ts
interface DevAIStore {
  conversations: Conversation[];
  activeConversation: string | null;
  isGenerating: boolean;
  streamingContent: string;
  
  // Actions
  generate: (prompt: string, context?: AIContext) => Promise<GeneratedCode>;
  complete: (prefix: string, suffix: string) => Promise<string>;
  explain: (code: string) => Promise<string>;
  fix: (code: string, error: string) => Promise<string>;
  refactor: (code: string, instruction: string) => Promise<string>;
  generateTests: (code: string) => Promise<string>;
  generateDocs: (code: string) => Promise<string>;
  generateCommitMessage: (diff: string) => Promise<string>;
  generatePRDescription: (commits: Commit[]) => Promise<string>;
  chat: (message: string) => Promise<void>;
}

// stores/devCollabStore.ts
interface DevCollabStore {
  users: OnlineUser[];
  cursors: Map<string, CursorPosition>;
  following: string | null;
  
  // Actions
  updatePresence: (file: string, cursor: Position) => void;
  follow: (userId: string) => void;
  unfollow: () => void;
  startScreenShare: () => Promise<void>;
  startVideoCall: () => Promise<void>;
}

// stores/devTerminalStore.ts
interface DevTerminalStore {
  terminals: Terminal[];
  activeTerminal: string | null;
  
  // Actions
  createTerminal: (shell?: string) => Terminal;
  closeTerminal: (id: string) => void;
  sendInput: (id: string, data: string) => void;
  resize: (id: string, cols: number, rows: number) => void;
  clear: (id: string) => void;
}
```

---

## 15. Implementation Roadmap

### Phase 1: Core IDE (Weeks 1-4)
- [ ] Project creation (blank, template, import)
- [ ] Monaco editor integration
- [ ] File tree & file operations
- [ ] Multi-tab editing
- [ ] Basic syntax highlighting

### Phase 2: Container Runtime (Weeks 5-7)
- [ ] Dev container provisioning
- [ ] Terminal (xterm.js)
- [ ] Dev server auto-detect & start
- [ ] Live preview
- [ ] Port forwarding

### Phase 3: Git Integration (Weeks 8-10)
- [ ] Git status & diff
- [ ] Stage/unstage/commit
- [ ] Branch management
- [ ] Push/pull operations
- [ ] Merge conflict UI

### Phase 4: GitHub Integration (Weeks 11-14)
- [ ] GitHub OAuth
- [ ] Repo import/clone
- [ ] Pull request management
- [ ] Issue tracking
- [ ] GitHub Actions viewer
- [ ] Webhooks

### Phase 5: AI Features (Weeks 15-18)
- [ ] Inline completion
- [ ] AI chat panel
- [ ] Code generation
- [ ] Explain/fix/refactor
- [ ] Commit message generation
- [ ] PR description generation
- [ ] Project generation from prompt

### Phase 6: Deployment (Weeks 19-21)
- [ ] One-click deploy (FooHut)
- [ ] Multi-environment support
- [ ] Deploy previews for PRs
- [ ] Environment variables
- [ ] Custom domains
- [ ] Third-party providers

### Phase 7: Collaboration (Weeks 22-24)
- [ ] Real-time presence
- [ ] Collaborative editing
- [ ] Following mode
- [ ] Comments
- [ ] Video/audio chat
- [ ] Screen sharing

---

## 16. Success Metrics

| Metric | Target | Measurement |
|--------|--------|-------------|
| Time to first preview | <60 seconds | New project to running preview |
| AI generation accuracy | >90% | Working code on first try |
| GitHub sync latency | <2 seconds | Push/pull operations |
| Container startup | <15 seconds | Cold start to running |
| Deployment time | <60 seconds | Commit to live |
| Collaboration latency | <100ms | Keystroke to other users |
| Daily active users | >10K | Monthly growth target |
| Projects created | >50K | Total projects |
